For example, a consumer\n    73→ * which is at position 5 has consumed records with offsets 0 through 4 and will next receive the record with offset 5.\n    74→ * Note that offsets are not guaranteed to be consecutive (such as compacted topic or when records have been produced\n    75→ * using transactions). See <a href=\"#multithreaded\">Multi-threaded Processing</a> for more details.\n *\n * <h3>Cross-Version Compatibility</h3>\n * This client can communicate with brokers that are version 0.10.0 or newer. This offset acts as a unique identifier of\n * a record within that partition, and also denotes the position of the consumer in the partition. For example, a consumer\n * which is at position 5 has consumed records with offsets 0 through 4 and will next receive the record with offset 5.\n * Note that offsets are not guaranteed to be consecutive (such as compacted topic or when records have been produced\n * using transactions). Interface\\n\\nThe legacy `kafka.consumer.ConsumerConnector` interface (from the old Scala-based high-level consumer API, which stored offsets in ZooKeeper and used `commitOffsets()`) is **not present** in any of the three repositories (`apache/kafka` at kafka--0753c489, `apache/flink` at flink--0cc95fcc, or `apache/camel` at camel--1006f047). This old API was deprecated and removed from Kafka 2.0. No Java files implementing `ConsumerConnector` were found.\\n\\n## New KafkaConsumer API Implementations\\n\\n### apache/kafka (kafka--0753c489)\\n\\nThe new consumer API is built around the `Consumer<K,V>` interface (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/Consumer.java`). Key implementations:\\n\\n1. **`KafkaConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/KafkaConsumer.java`) — The public-facing class that `implements Consumer<K,V>`. It delegates all operations to an internal `ConsumerDelegate<K,V>` (either `ClassicKafkaConsumer` or `AsyncKafkaConsumer`) chosen at construction time based on the `group.protocol` configuration.\\n\\n2. **`ClassicKafkaConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ClassicKafkaConsumer.java`) — `implements ConsumerDelegate<K,V>`. Uses the classic consumer group protocol (heartbeat-based). Offset management is handled synchronously on the calling thread via `ConsumerCoordinator.commitOffsetsSync()` / `commitOffsetsAsync()`, which send `OffsetCommitRequest` RPCs to the broker's `__consumer_offsets` topic. Auto-commit is triggered inside `poll()` via `maybeAutoCommitOffsetsAsync()`.\\n\\n3. **`AsyncKafkaConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AsyncKafkaConsumer.java`) — `implements ConsumerDelegate<K,V>`. Uses the new consumer group protocol (KIP-848). Offset management is event-driven: commit requests are posted as events to a `ConsumerNetworkThread` background thread, where `CommitRequestManager` processes them asynchronously. This decouples commit I/O from the application thread.\\n\\n4. **`MockConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/MockConsumer.java`) — `implements Consumer<K,V>`, used for testing.\\n\\n### apache/camel (camel--1006f047)\\n\\nThe Camel Kafka integration uses the new `KafkaConsumer` API (not the legacy `ConsumerConnector`):\\n\\n- **`KafkaConsumer.java`** (`components/camel-kafka/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/kafka/KafkaConsumer.java`) — Camel's consumer component, extends `DefaultConsumer`. It spawns `KafkaFetchRecords` threads that use the new `org.apache.kafka.clients.consumer.KafkaConsumer`.\\n\\n- **`KafkaFetchRecords.java`** (`components/camel-kafka/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/kafka/KafkaFetchRecords.java`) — The fetch loop using `KafkaConsumer.poll()`. Delegates offset commit decisions to a `CommitManager`.\\n\\n- **`AsyncCommitManager.java`** / **`SyncCommitManager.java`** (`components/camel-kafka/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/kafka/consumer/`) — Camel-level wrappers over `commitAsync()` and `commitSync()` of the new KafkaConsumer API.\\n\\n## Key Behavioral Differences in Offset Management\\n\\n| Aspect | Old ConsumerConnector (removed) | New KafkaConsumer — ClassicKafkaConsumer | New KafkaConsumer — AsyncKafkaConsumer |\\n|---|---|---|---|\\n| Offset storage | ZooKeeper | Kafka `__consumer_offsets` topic | Kafka `__consumer_offsets` topic |\\n| Commit API | `commitOffsets()` | `commitSync()` / `commitAsync()` | `commitSync()` / `commitAsync()` (event-driven) |\\n| Auto-commit | Background thread, ZK writes | Called within `poll()` via `ConsumerCoordinator.maybeAutoCommitOffsetsAsync()` | Managed by `CommitRequestManager` in dedicated `ConsumerNetworkThread` |\\n| Thread model | Multi-threaded (streams per partition) | Single-threaded (not thread-safe) | Single application thread + background network thread |\\n| Commit blocking | N/A | `commitSync()` blocks the calling thread | `commitSync()` posts event, waits on future; background thread executes |\\n\\nThe critical shift from old to new: offsets moved from ZooKeeper to a Kafka-native topic, the multi-threaded stream model was replaced by a single-threaded poll loop, and manual offset control (`commitSync`/`commitAsync`) became the recommended pattern for exactly-once semantics.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":404,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2092,"cache_read_input_tokens":48034,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":2092,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6c5e8ca4-af07-469f-a36a-4c62f0b3b823","uuid":"d3738c5d-598b-4cff-9c86-b9cc77030b55"}

Interface\\n\\nThe legacy `kafka.consumer.ConsumerConnector` interface (from the old Scala-based high-level consumer API, which stored offsets in ZooKeeper and used `commitOffsets()`) is **not present** in any of the three repositories (`apache/kafka` at kafka--0753c489, `apache/flink` at flink--0cc95fcc, or `apache/camel` at camel--1006f047). This old API was deprecated and removed from Kafka 2.0. No Java files implementing `ConsumerConnector` were found.\\n\\n## New KafkaConsumer API Implementations\\n\\n### apache/kafka (kafka--0753c489)\\n\\nThe new consumer API is built around the `Consumer<K,V>` interface (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/Consumer.java`). Key implementations:\\n\\n1. **`KafkaConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/KafkaConsumer.java`) — The public-facing class that `implements Consumer<K,V>`. It delegates all operations to an internal `ConsumerDelegate<K,V>` (either `ClassicKafkaConsumer` or `AsyncKafkaConsumer`) chosen at construction time based on the `group.protocol` configuration.\\n\\n2. **`ClassicKafkaConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ClassicKafkaConsumer.java`) — `implements ConsumerDelegate<K,V>`. Uses the classic consumer group protocol (heartbeat-based). Offset management is handled synchronously on the calling thread via `ConsumerCoordinator.commitOffsetsSync()` / `commitOffsetsAsync()`, which send `OffsetCommitRequest` RPCs to the broker's `__consumer_offsets` topic. Auto-commit is triggered inside `poll()` via `maybeAutoCommitOffsetsAsync()`.\\n\\n3. **`AsyncKafkaConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AsyncKafkaConsumer.java`) — `implements ConsumerDelegate<K,V>`. Uses the new consumer group protocol (KIP-848). Offset management is event-driven: commit requests are posted as events to a `ConsumerNetworkThread` background thread, where `CommitRequestManager` processes them asynchronously. This decouples commit I/O from the application thread.\\n\\n4. **`MockConsumer.java`** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/MockConsumer.java`) — `implements Consumer<K,V>`, used for testing.\\n\\n### apache/camel (camel--1006f047)\\n\\nThe Camel Kafka integration uses the new `KafkaConsumer` API (not the legacy `ConsumerConnector`):\\n\\n- **`KafkaConsumer.java`** (`components/camel-kafka/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/kafka/KafkaConsumer.java`) — Camel's consumer component, extends `DefaultConsumer`. It spawns `KafkaFetchRecords` threads that use the new `org.apache.kafka.clients.consumer.KafkaConsumer`.\\n\\n- **`KafkaFetchRecords.java`** (`components/camel-kafka/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/kafka/KafkaFetchRecords.java`) — The fetch loop using `KafkaConsumer.poll()`. Delegates offset commit decisions to a `CommitManager`.\\n\\n- **`AsyncCommitManager.java`** / **`SyncCommitManager.java`** (`components/camel-kafka/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/kafka/consumer/`) — Camel-level wrappers over `commitAsync()` and `commitSync()` of the new KafkaConsumer API.\\n\\n## Key Behavioral Differences in Offset Management\\n\\n| Aspect | Old ConsumerConnector (removed) | New KafkaConsumer — ClassicKafkaConsumer | New KafkaConsumer — AsyncKafkaConsumer |\\n|---|---|---|---|\\n| Offset storage | ZooKeeper | Kafka `__consumer_offsets` topic | Kafka `__consumer_offsets` topic |\\n| Commit API | `commitOffsets()` | `commitSync()` / `commitAsync()` | `commitSync()` / `commitAsync()` (event-driven) |\\n| Auto-commit | Background thread, ZK writes | Called within `poll()` via `ConsumerCoordinator.maybeAutoCommitOffsetsAsync()` | Managed by `CommitRequestManager` in dedicated `ConsumerNetworkThread` |\\n| Thread model | Multi-threaded (streams per partition) | Single-threaded (not thread-safe) | Single application thread + background network thread |\\n| Commit blocking | N/A | `commitSync()` blocks the calling thread | `commitSync()` posts event, waits on future; background thread executes |\\n\\nThe critical shift from old to new: offsets moved from ZooKeeper to a Kafka-native topic, the multi-threaded stream model was replaced by a single-threaded poll loop, and manual offset control (`commitSync`/`commitAsync`) became the recommended pattern for exactly-once semantics.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
